INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_COL_YR_STATS (HOSP_CD,TBL_ID,COL_ID,COL_SEQ,CRIT_YR,ROW_CNT,PT_CNT,STATS_WORK_YMD,COLL_STRT_YMD,COLL_END_YMD,CRTN_DT )  SELECT  DISTINCT  A.HOSP_CD, A.TBL_ID, A.COL_ID, A.COL_SEQ, B.CRIT_YR, B.ROW_CNT, C.PT_CNT, CONVERT(NVARCHAR, GETDATE(), 112) AS STATS_WORK_YMD  ,'20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD,'20211231'  AS COLL_END_YMD,CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT  FROM (SELECT '9999' AS HOSP_CD, '98020' AS TBL_ID , '9802001' AS COL_ID, 1 AS COL_SEQ FROM OBSERVATION_PERIOD WHERE OBSERVATION_PERIOD_ID IS NOT NULL )  A  ,(SELECT SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),OBSERVATION_PERIOD_START_DATE,112),1,4) AS CRIT_YR, COUNT(*) AS ROW_CNT FROM OBSERVATION_PERIOD WHERE  OBSERVATION_PERIOD_ID IS NOT NULL  AND OBSERVATION_PERIOD_START_DATE BETWEEN  '20100101' AND '20211231' GROUP BY SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),OBSERVATION_PERIOD_START_DATE,112),1,4)) B  ,(SELECT  C1.CRIT_YR, COUNT(*) AS PT_CNT FROM (SELECT SUBSTRING (CONVERT(CHAR(8),OBSERVATION_PERIOD_START_DATE,112),1,4) AS CRIT_YR , PERSON_ID  FROM OBSERVATION_PERIOD  WHERE OBSERVATION_PERIOD_ID IS NOT NULL  AND OBSERVATION_PERIOD_START_DATE BETWEEN  '20100101' AND '20211231' GROUP BY SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),OBSERVATION_PERIOD_START_DATE,112),1,4), PERSON_ID) C1  GROUP BY CRIT_YR) C WHERE B.CRIT_YR = C.CRIT_YR ORDER BY B.CRIT_YR ASC ;

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_COL_YR_STATS (HOSP_CD,TBL_ID,COL_ID,COL_SEQ,CRIT_YR,ROW_CNT,PT_CNT,STATS_WORK_YMD,COLL_STRT_YMD,COLL_END_YMD,CRTN_DT )  SELECT  DISTINCT  A.HOSP_CD, A.TBL_ID, A.COL_ID, A.COL_SEQ, B.CRIT_YR, B.ROW_CNT, C.PT_CNT, CONVERT(NVARCHAR, GETDATE(), 112) AS STATS_WORK_YMD  ,'20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD,'20211231'  AS COLL_END_YMD,CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT  FROM (SELECT '9999' AS HOSP_CD, '98060' AS TBL_ID , '9806020' AS COL_ID, 20 AS COL_SEQ FROM DRUG_EXPOSURE WHERE DRUG_SOURCE_VALUE IS NOT NULL )  A  ,(SELECT SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),DRUG_EXPOSURE_START_DATE,112),1,4) AS CRIT_YR, COUNT(*) AS ROW_CNT FROM DRUG_EXPOSURE WHERE  DRUG_SOURCE_VALUE IS NOT NULL  AND DRUG_EXPOSURE_START_DATE BETWEEN  '20100101' AND '20211231' GROUP BY SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),DRUG_EXPOSURE_START_DATE,112),1,4)) B  ,(SELECT  C1.CRIT_YR, COUNT(*) AS PT_CNT FROM (SELECT SUBSTRING (CONVERT(CHAR(8),DRUG_EXPOSURE_START_DATE,112),1,4) AS CRIT_YR , PERSON_ID  FROM DRUG_EXPOSURE  WHERE DRUG_SOURCE_VALUE IS NOT NULL  AND DRUG_EXPOSURE_START_DATE BETWEEN  '20100101' AND '20211231' GROUP BY SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),DRUG_EXPOSURE_START_DATE,112),1,4), PERSON_ID) C1  GROUP BY CRIT_YR) C WHERE B.CRIT_YR = C.CRIT_YR ORDER BY B.CRIT_YR ASC ;
